5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org

file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of findings:

## Pod Security Context Validation in Kubernetes v1.32.0

Validation is implemented at three layers:

### 1. API-Level Validation (`pkg/apis/core/validation/validation.go`)
- **`ValidateSecurityContext`** — validates container-level `SecurityContext`, including the `privileged` field (gated by `capabilities.Get().AllowPrivileged`)
- **`validatePodSpecSecurityContext`** — validates pod-level `PodSecurityContext` (runAsNonRoot, seccompProfile)
- **`validateSeccompProfileField`**, **`ValidateSeccompProfile`**, **`validateSeccompProfileType`** — validate seccomp profile type/annotation values

### 2. Pod Security Admission Policy (`staging/src/k8s.io/pod-security-admission/policy/`)
| File | Key symbols | What it checks |
|---|---|---|
| `check_runAsNonRoot.go` | `CheckRunAsNonRoot`, `runAsNonRoot_1_0` | Requires `runAsNonRoot=true` (restricted level) |
| `check_privileged.go` | `CheckPrivileged`, `privileged_1_0` | Forbids `privileged=true` (baseline level) |
| `check_capabilities_baseline.go` | `CheckCapabilitiesBaseline`, `capabilitiesBaseline_1_0` | Limits allowed added capabilities (baseline) |
| `check_capabilities_restricted.go` | `CheckCapabilitiesRestricted`, `capabilitiesRestricted_1_22/25` | Requires dropping ALL capabilities (restricted) |
| `check_seccompProfile_baseline.go` | `seccompProfileBaseline_1_0/1_19` | Forbids known-bad seccomp profiles (baseline) |
| `check_seccompProfile_restricted.go` | `CheckSeccompProfileRestricted`, `seccompProfileRestricted_1_19/1_25` | Requires RuntimeDefault or Localhost seccomp (restricted) |

### 3. Kubelet Runtime Enforcement (`pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/`)
- **`security_context_others.go`** — `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` for Linux containers
-

Pod Security Admission (PSA) policy checks** (`staging/src/k8s.io/pod-security-admission/policy/`):\\n- `check_runAsNonRoot.go`: `CheckRunAsNonRoot()` and `runAsNonRoot_1_0()` enforce `runAsNonRoot=true` as a restricted-level policy check.\\n- `check_privileged.go`: `CheckPrivileged()` and `privileged_1_0()` forbid `privileged=true` as a baseline-level check.\\n- `check_capabilities_baseline.go`: `CheckCapabilitiesBaseline()` and `capabilitiesBaseline_1_0()` restrict which capabilities may be added (baseline level).\\n- `check_capabilities_restricted.go`: `CheckCapabilitiesRestricted()`, `capabilitiesRestricted_1_22()`, `capabilitiesRestricted_1_25()` require dropping ALL capabilities (restricted level).\\n- `check_seccompProfile_baseline.go`: `seccompProfileBaseline_1_0()` and `seccompProfileBaseline_1_19()` enforce baseline seccomp profile constraints (forbids known-bad profiles).\\n- `check_seccompProfile_restricted.go`: `CheckSeccompProfileRestricted()`, `seccompProfileRestricted_1_19()`, `seccompProfileRestricted_1_25()` enforce restricted seccomp profile requirements (RuntimeDefault or Localhost).\\n- `checks.go`: defines the `Check`, `CheckResult`, and `CheckPodFn` types used by all policy checks.\\n- `helpers.go`: provides `RelaxPolicyForUserNamespacePods` helper used by runAsNonRoot and runAsUser checks.\\n\\n**3. Kubelet runtime enforcement** (`pkg/kubelet/kuberuntime/`):\\n- `security_context_others.go`: `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` enforces the runAsNonRoot constraint at container start time on Linux/non-Windows by inspecting the image's UID.\\n- `security_context_windows.go`: `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` enforces the runAsNonRoot constraint on Windows containers.\\n- `kuberuntime_container.go`: calls `verifyRunAsNonRoot()` during container config generation.\\n- `security_context.go`: synthesizes the effective security context (including seccompProfile) applied to containers at runtime via `getSeccompProfile`.\"\n}\n",
